# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="5f21e-102">Types obsolètes dans le .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-103">Les tableaux de cet article, organisés par assembly, répertorient les types qui sont obsolètes dans le [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] et le [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-104">Utilisez les liens suivants pour consulter la liste des types obsolètes et des alternatives recommandées dans chaque assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-105">Ces types étant obsolètes, tous leurs membres le sont également.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-106">Pour obtenir la liste des membres obsolètes supplémentaires dans la bibliothèque de classes .NET Framework, consultez [Membres obsolètes](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="5f21e-924">Types obsolètes dans les assemblys Microsoft</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-924">Obsolete Types in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-925">Les sections suivantes répertorient les types obsolètes dans les assemblys Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-925">The following sections list the obsolete types in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-926">Il s'agit d'assemblys ayant un usage spécial, comme les assemblys qui ciblent un langage individuel (par exemple, Microsoft.JScript.dll ou Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-926">These assemblies are special-purpose assemblies such as assemblies that target an individual language (for example, Microsoft.JScript.dll or Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span></span>

<a name="IEHost"></a>
### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="5f21e-927">Assembly : IEHost.dll et IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-927">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-928">Les assemblys IEHost.dll et IEExec.exe ont été supprimés du .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-928">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-929">Tous leurs types et leurs membres sont obsolètes et ne sont pas pris en charge à partir de [!INCLUDE[net_v40_short](../../../includes/net-v40-short-md.md)].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-929">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported as of the [!INCLUDE[net_v40_short](../../../includes/net-v40-short-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-930">Ces assemblys ont été utilisés pour héberger des contrôles Windows Forms et exécuter des exécutables dans Internet Explorer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-930">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5f21e-931">Les alternatives recommandées incluent ClickOnce, des applications du navigateur XAML (XBAP) et Microsoft Silverlight.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5f21e-931">Recommended alternatives include ClickOnce, XAML browser applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
